<P class="p254 ft4">Article 9</P>
<P class="p255 ft4">Regulatory Barriers</P>
<P class="p256 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">The States Parties shall, when possible, and in conformity with their national law, reduce or remove regulatory barriers to the use of telecommunication resources for disaster mitigation and relief, including to the provision of telecommunication assistance.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p187 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">Regulatory barriers may include, but are not limited to:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p257 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">regulations restricting the import or export of telecommunication equipment;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p258 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft69">regulations restricting the use of telecommunication equipment or of </SPAN><NOBR>radio-frequency</NOBR> spectrum;</P>
<P class="p259 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">regulations restricting the movement of personnel who operate telecommunication equipment or who are essential to its effective use;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p260 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft69">regulations restricting the transit of telecommunication resources into, out of and through the territory of a State Party; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p261 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">delays in the administration of such regulations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p262 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">Reduction of regulatory barriers may take the form of, but shall not be limited to:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p237 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">revising regulations;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p263 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft69">exempting specified telecommunication resources from the application of those regulations during the use of such resources for disaster mitigation and relief;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p264 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">c)</SPAN><NOBR><SPAN class="ft67">pre-clearance</SPAN></NOBR> of telecommunication resources for use in disaster mitigation and relief, in compliance</P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t19">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td106"><SPAN class="p2 ft2">with those regulations;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td107"><SPAN class="p3 ft6">34</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_35">


<P class="p265 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29 <SPAN class="ft2">d) recognition of foreign </SPAN><NOBR><SPAN class="ft2">type-approval</SPAN></NOBR><SPAN class="ft2"> of </SPAN>Bilaga 1</P>
<P class="p266 ft2">telecommunication equipment and/or operating licenses;</P>
<P class="p267 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">expedited review of telecommunication resources for use in disaster mitigation and relief, in compliance with those regulations; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p268 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft82">temporary waiver of those regulations for the use of telecommunication resources for disaster mitigation and relief.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p232 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">Each State Party shall, at the request of any other State Party, and to the extent permitted by its national law, facilitate the transit into, out of and through its territory of personnel, equipment, materials and information involved in the use of telecommunication resources for disaster mitigation and relief.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p252 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">Each State Party shall notify the operational coordinator and the other States Parties, directly or through the operational coordinator, of:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p268 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">measures taken, pursuant to this Convention, for reducing or removing such regulatory barriers;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p267 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft69">procedures available, pursuant to this Convention, to States Parties, other States, </SPAN><NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entities and/or intergovernmental organizations for the exemption of specified telecommunication resources used for disaster mitigation and relief from the application of such regulations, <NOBR>pre-clearance</NOBR> or expedited review of such resources in compliance with applicable regulations, acceptance of foreign <NOBR>type-approval</NOBR> of such resources, or temporary waiver of regulations otherwise applicable to such resources; and</P>
<P class="p269 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">the terms, conditions and restrictions, if any, associated with the use of such procedures.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p270 ft56"><SPAN class="ft56">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">The operational coordinator shall regularly and expeditiously make available to the States Parties, to other States, to </SPAN><NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entities and to intergovernmental organizations an <NOBR>up-to-date</NOBR> listing of such measures, their scope, and the terms, conditions and restrictions, if any, associated with their use.</P>
<P class="p271 ft6">35</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_36">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p185 ft2">7. Nothing in. this Article shall permit the violation or abrogation of obligations and responsibilities imposed by national law, international law, or multilateral or bilateral agreements, including obligations and responsibilities concerning customs and export controls.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 1</P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p272 ft4">Article 10</P>
<P class="p273 ft4">Relationship to Other International Agreements</P>
<P class="p181 ft2">This Convention shall not affect the rights and obligations of States Parties deriving from other international agreements or international law.</P>
<P class="p274 ft4">Article 11</P>
<P class="p275 ft4">Dispute Settlement</P>
<P class="p181 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">In the event of a dispute between States Parties concerning the interpretation or application of this Convention, the States Parties to the dispute shall consult each other for the purpose of settling the dispute. Such consultation shall begin promptly upon the written declaration, delivered by one State Party to another State Party, of the existence of a dispute under this Convention. The State Party making such a written declaration of the existence of a dispute shall promptly deliver a copy of such declaration to the depositary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p276 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">If a dispute between States Parties cannot be settled within six</SPAN></P>
<P class="p28 ft2">(6) months of the date of delivery of the written declaration to a State Party to the dispute, the States Parties to the dispute may request any other State Party, State, <NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entity or intergovernmental organization to use its good offices to facilitate settlement of the dispute.</P>
<P class="p13 ft56"><SPAN class="ft56">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft74">If neither State Party seeks the good offices of another State Party, State, </SPAN><NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entity or intergovernmental organization, or if the exercise of good offices fails to facilitate a settlement of the dispute within six (6) months of the request for such good offices being made, then either State Party to the dispute may:</P>
<P class="p277 ft6">36</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_37">


<P class="p22 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p278 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">request that the dispute be submitted to binding </SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">Bilaga 1 </SPAN>arbitration; or</P>
<P class="p194 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft69">submit the dispute to the International Court of Justice for decision, provided that both States Parties to the dispute have, at the time of signing, ratifying or acceding to this Convention, or at any time thereafter, accepted the jurisdiction of the International Court of Justice in respect of such disputes.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p279 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft70">In the event that the respective States Parties to the dispute request that the dispute be submitted to binding arbitration and submit the dispute to the International Court of Justice for decision, the submission to the International Court of Justice shall have priority.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p280 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft72">In the case of a dispute between a State Party requesting telecommunication assistance and a </SPAN><NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entity or intergovernmental organization headquartered or domiciled outside of the territory of that State Party concerning the provision of telecommunication assistance under Article 4, the claim of the <NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entity or intergovernmental organization may be espoused directly by the State Party in which the non- State entity or intergovernmental organization is headquartered or domiciled as a <NOBR>State-to-State</NOBR> claim under this Article, provided that such espousal is not inconsistent with any other agreement between the State Party and the <NOBR>non-State</NOBR> entity or intergovernmental organization involved in the dispute.</P>
<P class="p281 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">When signing, ratifying, accepting, approving or acceding to this Convention, a State may declare that it does not consider itself bound by either or both of the dispute settlement procedures provided for in paragraph 3 above. The other States Parties shall not be bound by a dispute settlement procedure provided for in paragraph 3 with respect to a State Party for which such a declaration is in force.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p282 ft4">Article 12</P>
<P class="p283 ft4">Entry into Force</P>
<P class="p284 ft6">37</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_38">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p84 ft2">1. This Convention shall be open for signature by all States which are members of the United Nations or of the International Telecommunication Union at the Intergovernmental Conference on Emergency Telecommunications in Tampere on 18 June 1998, and thereafter at the headquarters of the United Nations, New York, from 22 June 1998 to 21 June 2003.</P>
<P class="p285 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft80">A State may express its consent to be bound by this Convention:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p237 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">by signature (definitive signature);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p236 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft69">by signature subject to ratification, acceptance or approval followed by deposit of an instrument of ratification, acceptance or approval; or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p261 ft2"><SPAN class="ft68">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft67">by deposit of an instrument of accession.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p170 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">The Convention shall enter into force thirty (30) days after the deposit of instruments of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession or definitive signature of thirty (30) States.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p212 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft80">For each State which signs definitively or deposits an instrument of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession, after the requirement set out in paragraph 3 of this Article has been fulfilled, this Convention shall enter into force thirty (30) days after the date of the definitive signature or consent to be bound.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p272 ft4">Article 13</P>
<P class="p189 ft4">Amendments</P>
<P class="p181 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">A State Party may propose amendments to this Convention by submitting such amendments to the depositary, which shall circulate them to the other States Parties for approval.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p173 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">The States Parties shall notify the depositary of their approval or disapproval of such proposed amendments within one hundred and eighty (180) days of their receipt.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p286 ft6">38</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_39">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p185 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">Any amendment approved by </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> of all States Parties shall be laid down in a Protocol which is open for signature at the depositary by all States Parties.</P>
<P class="p187 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">The Protocol shall enter into force in the same manner as this Convention. For each State which signs the Protocol definitively or deposits an instrument of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession, after the requirements for the entry into force of the Protocol have been fulfilled, the Protocol shall enter into force for such State thirty (30) days after the date of the definitive signature or consent to be bound.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 1</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p272 ft4">Article 14</P>
<P class="p287 ft4">Reservations</P>
<P class="p181 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft63">When definitively signing, ratifying or acceding to this Convention or any amendment hereto, a State Party may make reservations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p181 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">A State Party may at any time withdraw its prior reservation by written notification to the depositary. Such withdrawal of a reservation becomes effective immediately upon notification to the depositary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p288 ft4">Article 15</P>
<P class="p289 ft4">Denunciation</P>
<P class="p181 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft75">A State Party may denounce this Convention by written notification to the depositary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p175 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">Denunciation shall take effect ninety (90) days following the date of deposit of the written notification.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p290 ft6">39</P>
</DIV>

<P class="p300 ft88">ORGANISATION INTERNATIONALE DE TELECOMMUNICATIONS PAR SATELLITES</P>
<P class="p301 ft88">ORGANIZACION INTERNACIONAL DE TELECOMUNICACIONES POR SATELITE</P>

<P class="p22 ft6">Bilaga 2</P>
<P class="p303 ft2">Agreement Relating to the International Telecommunications Satellite Organisation</P>
<P class="p304 ft10">Includes the amendments to the Agreement approved by the Twenty- Fifth (Extraordinary) Assembly of Parties in Washington, D.C.,</P>
<P class="p305 ft10">on 17 November 2000.</P>
<P class="p306 ft6">41</P>

<DIV id="page_42">

<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td108"><SPAN class="p307 ft89">AGREEMENT RELATING TO THE INTERNATIONAL</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td108"><SPAN class="p308 ft89">TELECOMMUNICATIONS SATELLITE ORGANIZATION</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p309 ft7">PREAMBLE</P>
<P class="p310 ft7">The States Parties to this Agreement,</P>
<P class="p311 ft7">Considering the principle set forth in Resolution 1721 (XVI) of the General Assembly of the United Nations that communication by means of satellites should be available to the nations of the world as soon as practicable on a global and <NOBR>non-discriminatory</NOBR> basis,</P>
<P class="p312 ft7">Considering the relevant provisions of the Treaty on Principles Governing the Activities of States in the Exploration and Use of Outer Space, Including the Moon and Other Celestial Bodies, and in particular Article I, which states that outer space shall be used for the benefit and in the interests of all countries,</P>
<P class="p313 ft10">Recognizing that the International Telecommunications Satellite Organization has, in accordance with its original purpose, established a global satellite system for providing telecommunications services to all areas of the world, which has contributed to world peace and understanding,</P>
<P class="p314 ft7">Taking into account that the 24th Assembly of Parties of the International Telecommunications Satellite Organization decided to restructure and privatize by establishing a private company supervised by an intergovernmental organization,</P>
<P class="p315 ft90">Acknowledging that increased competition in the provision of telecommunications services has made it necessary for the International Telecommunications Satellite Organization to transfer its space system to the Company defined in Article 1(d) of this Agreement in order that the space system continues to be operated in a commercially viable manner,</P>
<P class="p316 ft7">Intending that the Company will honor the Core Principles set forth in Article III of this Agreement and will provide, on a commercial basis, the space segment required for international public telecommunications services of high quality and reliability,</P>
<P class="p317 ft10">Having determined that there is a need for an intergovernmental supervisory organization, to which any State member of the United Nations or the International Telecommunication Union may become a Party, to ensure that the Company fulfills the Core Principles on a continuing basis,</P>
<P class="p160 ft7">Agree as follows:</P>
<P class="p318 ft7">Definitions</P>
<P class="p319 ft7">ARTICLE I</P>
<P class="p5 ft7">For the purposes of this Agreement:</P>
<P class="p320 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">“Agreement” means the present agreement, including its Annex, and any amendments thereto, but excluding all titles of Articles, opened for signature by Governments at Washington on August 20, 1971, by which the international telecommunications satellite organization is established;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p321 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">“Space segment” means the telecommunications satellites, and the tracking, telemetry, command, control, monitoring and related facilities and equipment required to support the operation of these satellites;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p184 ft6">42</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_43">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t15">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p322 ft10">(c) “Telecommunications” means any transmission, emission or</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">reception of signs, signals, writing, images and sounds or intelligence of any</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">nature, by wire, radio, optical or other electromagnetic systems;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p323 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">“Company” means the private entity or entities established under the law of one or more States to which the international telecommunications satellite organization’s space system is transferred and includes their </SPAN><NOBR>successors-in-interest;</NOBR></P>
<P class="p324 ft42"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">“On a Commercial Basis” means in accordance with usual and customary commercial practice in the telecommunications industry;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p325 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">“Public telecommunications services” means fixed or mobile telecommunications services which can be provided by satellite and which are available for use by the public, such as telephony, telegraphy, telex, facsimile, data transmission, transmission of radio and television programs between approved earth stations having access to the Company’s space segment for further transmission to the public, and leased circuits for any of these purposes; but excluding those mobile services of a type not provided under the Interim Agreement and the Special Agreement prior to the opening for signature of this Agreement, which are provided through mobile stations operating directly to a satellite which is designed, in whole or in part, to provide services relating to the safety or flight control of aircraft or to aviation or maritime radio navigation;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p326 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">“Interim Agreement” means the Agreement Establishing Interim Arrangements for a Global Commercial Communications Satellite System signed by Governments at Washington on August 20, 1964;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p327 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">“Lifeline Connectivity Obligation” or “LCO” means the obligation assumed by the Company as set out in the LCO contract to provide continued telecommunications services to the LCO customer;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p328 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft95">“Special Agreement” means the agreement signed on August 20, 1964, by Governments or telecommunications entities designated by Governments, pursuant to the provisions of the Interim Agreement;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p329 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(j)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">“Public Services Agreement” means the legally binding instrument through which ITSO ensures that the Company honors the Core Principles;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p330 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">“Core Principles” means those principles set forth in Article</SPAN></P>
<P class="p331 ft7">III;</P>
<P class="p320 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(l)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">“Common Heritage” means those frequency assignments associated with orbital locations in the process of advanced publication, coordination or registered on behalf of the Parties with the International Telecommunication Union (“ITU”) in accordance with the provisions set forth in the ITU’s Radio Regulations which are transferred to a Party or Parties pursuant to Article XII;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p332 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(m)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft95">“Global coverage” means the maximum geographic coverage of the earth towards the northernmost and southernmost parallels visible from satellites deployed in geostationary orbital locations;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p333 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(n)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">“Global connectivity” means the interconnection capabilities available to the Company’s customers through the global coverage the Company provides in order to make communication possible within and between the five International Telecommunication Union regions defined by the plenipotentiary conference of the ITU, held in Montreux in 1965;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p334 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(o)</SPAN><NOBR><SPAN class="ft91">“Non-discriminatory</SPAN></NOBR> access” means fair and equal opportunity to access the Company’s system;</P>
<P class="p335 ft6">43</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_44">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t21">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p322 ft7">(p) “Party” means a State for which the Agreement has entered</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">into force or has been provisionally applied;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p336 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(q)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">“Property” includes every subject of whatever nature to which a right of ownership can attach, as well as contractual rights;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p337 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(r)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">“LCO customers” means all customers qualifying for and entering into LCO contracts; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p338 ft7"><SPAN class="ft42">(s)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">“Administration” means any governmental department or agency responsible for compliance with the obligations derived from the Constitution of the International Telecommunication Union, the Convention of the International Telecommunication Union, and its Administrative Regulations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p339 ft7">Establishment of ITSO</P>
<P class="p340 ft7">ARTICLE II</P>
<P class="p341 ft10">The Parties, with full regard for the principles set forth in the Preamble to this Agreement, establish the International Telecommunications Satellite Organization, herein referred to as “ITSO”.</P>
<P class="p342 ft7">Main Purpose and Core Principles of ITSO</P>
<P class="p343 ft7">ARTICLE III</P>
<P class="p344 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Taking into account the establishment of the Company, the main purpose of ITSO is to ensure, through the Public Services Agreement, that the Company provides, on a commercial basis, international public telecommunications services, in order to ensure performance of the Core Principles.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p345 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Core Principles are:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p346 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">maintain global connectivity and global coverage;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p347 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">serve its lifeline connectivity customers; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p347 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(iii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">provide </SPAN><NOBR>non-discriminatory</NOBR> access to the</P>
<P class="p183 ft7">Company’s system.</P>
<P class="p348 ft7">Covered Domestic Public Telecommunications Services</P>
<P class="p349 ft7">ARTICLE IV</P>
<P class="p350 ft7">The following shall be considered for purposes of applying Article III on the same basis as international public telecommunications services:</P>
<P class="p351 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">domestic public telecommunications services between areas separated by areas not under the jurisdiction of the State concerned, or between areas separated by the high seas; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p352 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">domestic public telecommunications services between areas which are not linked by any terrestrial wideband facilities and which are separated by natural barriers of such an exceptional nature that they impede the viable establishment of terrestrial wideband facilities between such areas, provided that the appropriate approval has been given.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p353 ft6">44</P>

<P class="p358 ft7">Financial Principles</P>
<P class="p359 ft7">ARTICLE VII</P>
<P class="p360 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">ITSO will be financed for the twelve year period established in Article XXI by the retention of certain financial assets at the time of transfer of ITSO’s space system to the Company.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p361 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">In the event ITSO continues beyond twelve years, ITSO shall obtain funding through the Public Services Agreement</SPAN></P>
<P class="p362 ft7">Structure of ITSO</P>
<P class="p363 ft7">ARTICLE VIII</P>
<P class="p176 ft7">ITSO shall have the following organs:</P>
<P class="p364 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">the Assembly of Parties; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p365 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">an executive organ, headed by the Director General, responsible to the Assembly of Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p366 ft7">Assembly of Parties</P>
<P class="p367 ft7">ARTICLF IX</P>
<P class="p368 ft7">(a) The Assembly of Parties shall be composed of all the Parties and shall he the principal organ of ITSO.</P>
<P class="p335 ft6">45</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_46">
<DIV id="dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="GR032946x1.jpg/" id="img1">
</DIV>


<DIV class="dclr"></DIV>
<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p369 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Assembly of Parties shall give consideration to general policy and </SPAN><NOBR>long-term</NOBR> objectives of ITSO.</P>
<P class="p370 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">The Assembly of Parties shall give consideration to matters which are primarily of interest to the Parties as sovereign States, and in particular ensure that the Company provides, on a commercial basis, international public telecommunications services, in order to:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p371 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">maintain global connectivity and global coverage;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p372 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">serve its lifeline connectivity customers; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p373 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(iii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">provide </SPAN><NOBR>non-discriminatory</NOBR> access to the</P>
<P class="p51 ft7">Company’s system.</P>
<P class="p374 ft7">(d) The Assembly of Parties shall have the following functions and powers:</P>
<P class="p375 ft10">(i) to direct the executive organ of ITSO as it deems appropriate, in particular regarding the executive organ’s review of the activities of the Company that directly relate to the Core Principles;</P>
<P class="p376 ft10">(ii) to consider and take decisions on proposals for amending this Agreement in accordance with Article XV of this Agreement;</P>
<P class="p377 ft7">(iii) to appoint and remove the Director General in accordance with Article X;</P>
<P class="p378 ft7">(iv) to consider and decide on reports submitted by the Director General that relate to the Company’s observance of the Core Principles;</P>
<P class="p379 ft7">(v) to consider and, in its discretion, take decisions on recommendations from the Director General;</P>
<P class="p380 ft7">(vi) to take decisions, pursuant to paragraph (b) of Article XIV of this Agreement, in connection with the withdrawal of a Party from ITSO;</P>
<P class="p381 ft7">(vii) to decide upon questions concerning formal relationships between ITSO and States, whether Parties or not, or international organizations;</P>
<P class="p382 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(viii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">to consider complaints submitted to it by Parties;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p372 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(ix)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">to consider issues pertaining to the Parties’</SPAN></P>
<P class="p51 ft7">Common Heritage;</P>
<P class="p383 ft7">(x) to take decisions concerning the approval referred to in paragraph (b) of Article IV of this Agreement;</P>
<P class="p384 ft7">(xi) to consider and approve the budget of ITSO for such period as agreed to by the Assembly of Parties;</P>
<P class="p385 ft10">(xii) to take any necessary decisions with respect to contingencies that may arise outside of the approved budget;</P>
<P class="p386 ft7">(xiii) to appoint an auditor to review the expenditures and accounts of ITSO;</P>
<P class="p387 ft7">(xiv) to select the legal experts referred to in Article 3 of Annex A to this Agreement;</P>
<P class="p388 ft7">(xv) to determine the conditions under which the Director General may commence an arbitration proceeding against the Company pursuant to the Public Services Agreement;</P>
<P class="p389 ft10">(xvi) to decide upon amendments proposed to the Public Services Agreement; and (xvii) to exercise any other functions conferred upon it under any other Article of this Agreement.</P>
<P class="p390 ft98">(e) The Assembly of Parties shall meet in ordinary session every two years beginning no later than twelve months after the transfer of ITSO’s space system to the Company. In addition to the ordinary meetings of the</P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 2</P>

<P class="p391 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">A quorum for any meeting of the Assembly of Parties shall consist of representatives of a majority of the Parties. Decisions on matters of substance shall be taken by an affirmative vote cast by at least </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> of the Parties whose representatives are present and voting. Decisions on procedural matters shall be taken by an affirmative vote cast by a simple majority of the Parties whose representatives are present and voting. Disputes whether a specific matter is procedural or substantive shall be decided by a vote cast by a simple majority of the Parties whose representatives are present and voting. Parties shall be afforded an opportunity to vote by proxy or other means as deemed appropriate by the Assembly of Parties and shall be provided with necessary information sufficiently in advance of the meeting of the Assembly of Parties.</P>
<P class="p392 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">For any meeting of the Assembly of Parties, each Party shall</SPAN></P>
<P class="p331 ft7">have one vote.</P>
<P class="p393 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Assembly of Parties shall adopt its own rules of procedure, which shall include provision for the election of a Chairman and other officers as well as provisions for participation and voting.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p394 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">Each Party shall meet its own costs of representation at a meeting of the Assembly of Parties. Expenses</SPAN></P>
<P class="p395 ft7">of meetings of the Assembly of Parties shall he regarded as an administrative cost of ITSO.</P>
<P class="p396 ft7">Director General</P>
<P class="p340 ft7">ARTICLE X</P>
<P class="p397 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The executive organ shall be headed by the Director General who shall be directly responsible to the Assembly of Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p398 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Director General shall</SPAN></P>
<P class="p399 ft7">(i) be the chief executive and the legal representative of ITSO and shall be responsible for the performance of all management functions, including the exercise of rights under contract;</P>
<P class="p400 ft7">(ii) act in accordance with the policies and directives of the Assembly of Parties; and</P>
<P class="p401 ft7">(iii) be appointed by the Assembly of Parties for a term of four years or such other period as the Assembly of Parties decides. The Director General may be removed from office for cause by the Assembly of Parties. No person shall be appointed as Director General for more than eight years.</P>
<P class="p402 ft90">(c) The paramount consideration in the appointment of the Director General and in the selection of other personnel of the executive organ shall be the necessity of ensuring the highest standards of integrity, competency and efficiency, with consideration given to the possible advantages of recruitment and deployment on a regionally and</P>
<P class="p184 ft6">47</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_48">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t15">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">geographically diverse basis. The Director General and the personnel of the</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">executive organ shall refrain from any action incompatible with their</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">responsibilities to ITSO.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p403 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">The Director General shall, subject to the guidance and instructions of the Assembly of Parties, determine the structure, staff levels and standard terms of employment of officials and employees, and shall appoint the personnel of the executive organ. The Director General may select consultants and other advisers to the executive organ.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p404 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Director General shall supervise the Company’s adherence to the Core Principles.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p330 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Director General shall</SPAN></P>
<P class="p346 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">monitor the Company’s adherence to the Core</SPAN></P>
<P class="p23 ft7">Principle to serve LCO customers by honoring LCO contracts;</P>
<P class="p405 ft7">(ii) consider the decisions taken by the Company with respect to petitions for eligibility to enter into an LCO contract;</P>
<P class="p406 ft7">(iii) assist LCO customers in resolving their disputes with the Company by providing conciliation services; and</P>
<P class="p407 ft7">(iv) in the event an LCO customer decides to initiate an arbitration proceeding against the Company, provide advice on the selection of consultants and arbiters.</P>
<P class="p408 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Director General shall report to the Parties on the matters referred to in paragraphs (d) through (f).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p409 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Pursuant to the terms to be established by the Assembly of Parties, the Director General may commence arbitration proceedings against the Company pursuant to the Public Services Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p410 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">The Director General shall deal with the Company in accordance with the Public Services Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p411 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(j)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft95">The Director General, on behalf of ITSO, shall consider all issues arising from the Parties’ Common Heritage and shall communicate the views of the Parties to the Notifying Administration(s).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p412 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">When the Director General is of the view that a Party’s failure to take action pursuant to Article XI(c) has impaired the Company’s ability to comply with the Core Principles, the Director General shall contact that Party to seek a resolution of the situation and may, consistent with the conditions established by the Assembly of Parties pursuant to Article IX(e), convene an extraordinary meeting of the Assembly of Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p413 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(l)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">The Assembly of Parties shall designate a senior officer of the executive organ to serve as the Acting Director General whenever the Director General is absent or is unable to discharge his duties, or if the office of Director General should become vacant. The Acting Director General shall have the capacity to exercise all the powers of the Director General pursuant to this Agreement. In the event of a vacancy, the Acting Director General shall serve in that capacity until the assumption of office by a Director General appointed and confirmed, as expeditiously as possible, in accordance with subparagraph (b) (iii) of this Article.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p414 ft7">Rights and Obligations of Parties</P>
<P class="p349 ft7">ARTICLE XI</P>
<P class="p415 ft10">(a) The Parties shall exercise their rights and meet their obligations under this Agreement in a manner fully consistent with and in</P>
<P class="p184 ft6">48</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_49">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t21">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">furtherance of the principles stated in the Preamble, the Core Principles in</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">Article III and other provisions of this Agreement.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p416 ft98"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft100">All Parties shall be allowed to attend and participate in all conferences and meetings, in which they are entitled to be represented in accordance with any provisions of this Agreement, as well as any other meeting called by or held under the auspices of ITSO, in accordance with the arrangements made by ITSO for such meetings regardless of where they may take place. The executive organ shall ensure that arrangements with the host Party for each such conference or meeting shall include a provision for the admission to the host country and sojourn for the duration of such conference or meeting, of representatives of all Parties entitled to attend.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p417 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">All Parties shall take the actions required, in a transparent, </SPAN><NOBR>non-discriminatory,</NOBR> and competitively neutral manner, under applicable domestic procedure and pertinent international agreements to which they are party, so that the Company may fulfill the Core Principles.</P>
<P class="p418 ft7">Frequency Assignments</P>
<P class="p419 ft7">ARTICLE XII</P>
<P class="p420 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The Parties of ITSO shall retain the orbital locations and frequency assignments in process of coordination or registered on behalf of the Parties with the ITU pursuant to the provisions set forth in the ITU’s Radio Regulations until such time as the selected Notifying Administration(s) has provided its notification to the Depositary that it has approved, accepted or ratified the present Agreement. The Parties shall select among the ITSO members a Party to represent all ITSO member Parties with the ITU during the period in which the Parties of ITSO retain such assignments.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p421 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The Party selected pursuant to paragraph (a) to represent all Parties during the period in which ITSO retains the assignments shall, upon the receipt of the notification by the Depositary of the approval, acceptance or ratification of the present Agreement by a Party selected by the Assembly of Parties to act as a Notifying Administration for the Company, transfer such assignments to the selected Notifying Administration(s).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p422 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Any Party selected to act as the Company’s Notifying Administration shall, under applicable domestic procedure:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p423 ft7">(i) authorize the use of such frequency assignment by the Company so that the Core Principles may be fulfilled; and</P>
<P class="p424 ft7">(ii) in the event that such use is no longer authorized, or the Company no longer requires such frequency assignment(s), cancel such frequency assignment under the procedures of the ITU.</P>
<P class="p425 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Notwithstanding any other provision of this Agreement, in the event a Party selected to act as a Notifying Administration for the Company ceases to be a member of ITSO pursuant to Article XIV, such Party shall be bound and subject to all relevant provisions set forth in this Agreement and in the ITU’s Radio Regulations until the frequency assignments are transferred to another Party in accordance with ITU procedures.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p426 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Each Party selected to act as a Notifying Administration pursuant to paragraph (c) shall:</SPAN></P>

<P class="p427 ft7">ITSO Headquarters, Privileges, Exemptions, Immunities</P>
<P class="p428 ft7">ARTICLE XIII</P>
<P class="p429 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The headquarters of ITSO shall be in Washington, D.C. unless otherwise determined by the Assembly of Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p430 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Within the scope of activities authorized by this Agreement, ITSO and its property shall be exempt in all States Party to this Agreement from all national income and direct national property taxation. Each Party undertakes to use its best endeavors to bring about, in accordance with the applicable domestic procedure, such further exemption of ITSO and its property from income and direct property taxation, and customs duties, as is desirable, bearing in mind the particular nature of ITSO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p431 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Each Party other than the Party in whose territory the headquarters of ITSO is located shall grant in accordance with the Protocol referred to in this paragraph, and the Party in whose territory the headquarters of ITSO is located shall grant in accordance with the Headquarters Agreement referred to in this paragraph, the appropriate privileges, exemptions and immunities to ITSO, to its officers, and to those categories of its employees specified in such Protocol and Headquarters Agreement, to Parties and representatives of Parties. In particular, each Party shall grant to these individuals immunity from legal process in respect of acts done or words written or spoken in the exercise of their functions and within the limits of their duties, to the extent and in the cases to be provided for in the Headquarters Agreement and Protocol referred to in this paragraph. The Party in whose territory the headquarters of ITSO is located shall, as soon as possible, conclude a Headquarters Agreement with ITSO covering privileges, exemptions and immunities. The other Parties shall, also as soon as possible, conclude a Protocol covering privileges, exemptions and immunities. The Headquarters Agreement and the Protocol shall be independent of this Agreement and each shall prescribe the conditions of its termination.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p436 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Upon the receipt by the Depositary or the executive organ, as the case may be, of notice of decision to withdraw pursuant to subparagraph (a)(i) of this Article, the Party giving notice shall cease to have any rights of representation and any voting rights in the Assembly of Parties, and shall incur no obligation or liability after the receipt of the notice.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p437 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">If the Assembly of Parties, pursuant to paragraph (b) of this Article, deems a Party to have withdrawn from ITSO, that Party shall incur no obligation or liability after such decision.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p438 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">No Party shall be required to withdraw from ITSO as a direct result of any change in the status of that Party with regard to the United Nations or the International Telecommunication Union.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p439 ft7">Amendment</P>
<P class="p419 ft7">ARTICLE XV</P>
<P class="p440 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Any Party may propose amendments to this Agreement. Proposed amendments shall be submitted to the executive organ, which shall distribute them promptly to all Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p441 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The Assembly of Parties shall consider each proposed amendment at its first ordinary meeting following its distribution by the executive organ, or at an earlier extraordinary meeting convened in accordance with the procedures of Article IX of this Agreement, provided that the proposed amendment has been distributed by the executive organ at least ninety days before the opening date of the meeting.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p442 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">The Assembly of Parties shall take decisions on each proposed amendment in accordance with the provisions relating to quorum and voting contained in Article IX of this Agreement. It may modify any proposed amendment, distributed in accordance with paragraph (b) of this</SPAN></P>
<P class="p227 ft6">51</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_52">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t21">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">Article, and may also take decisions on any amendment not so distributed</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">but directly consequential to a proposed or modified amendment.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p443 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">An amendment which has been approved by the Assembly of Parties shall enter into force in accordance with paragraph (e) of this Article after the Depositary has received notice of approval, acceptance or ratification of the amendment from </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> of the States which were Parties as of the date upon which the amendment was approved by the Assembly of Parties.</P>
<P class="p444 ft42"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">The Depositary shall notify all the Parties as soon as it has received the acceptances, approvals or ratifications required by paragraph</SPAN></P>
<P class="p445 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">of this Article for the entry into force of an amendment. Ninety days after the date of issue of this notification, the amendment shall enter into force for all Parties, including those that have not yet accepted, approved, or ratified it and have not withdrawn from ITSO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p446 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft95">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraphs (d) and (e) of this Article, an amendment shall not enter into force less than eight months after the date it has been approved by the Assembly of Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p447 ft7">Settlement of Disputes</P>
<P class="p448 ft7">ARTICLE XVI</P>
<P class="p449 ft90"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">All legal disputes arising in connection with the rights and obligations under this Agreement between Parties with respect to each other, or between ITSO and one or more Parties, if not otherwise settled within a reasonable time, shall be submitted to arbitration in accordance with the provisions of Annex A to this Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p450 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">All legal disputes arising in connection with the rights and obligations under this Agreement between a Party and a State which has ceased to be a Party or between ITSO and a State which has ceased to be a Party, and which arise after the State ceased to be a Party, if not otherwise settled within a reasonable time, shall be submitted to arbitration in accordance with the provisions of Annex A to this Agreement, provided that the State which has ceased to be a Party so agrees. If a State ceases to be a Party, after a dispute in which it is a disputant has been submitted to arbitration pursuant to paragraph (a) of this Article, the arbitration shall be continued and concluded.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p451 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">All legal disputes arising as a result of agreements between ITSO and any Party shall be subject to the provisions on settlement of disputes contained in such agreements. In the absence of such provisions, such disputes, if not otherwise settled, may be submitted to arbitration in accordance with the provisions of Annex A to this Agreement if the disputants so agree.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p452 ft7">Signature</P>
<P class="p453 ft7">ARTICLE XVII</P>
<P class="p454 ft7">(a) This Agreement shall be open for signature at Washington from August 20, 1971 until it enters into force, or until a period of nine months has elapsed, whichever occurs first:</P>

<P class="p457 ft7">Entry Into Force</P>
<P class="p458 ft7">ARTICLE XVIII</P>
<P class="p459 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">This Agreement shall enter into force sixty days after the date on which it has been signed not subject to ratification, acceptance or approval, or has been ratified, accepted, approved or acceded to, by twothirds of the States which were parties to the Interim Agreement as of the date upon which this Agreement is opened for signature, provided that such </SPAN><NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> include parties to the Interim Agreement which then held at least <NOBR>two-thirds</NOBR> of the quotas under the Special Agreement. Notwithstanding the foregoing provisions, this Agreement shall not enter into force less than eight months or more than eighteen months after the date it is opened for signature.</P>
<P class="p460 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">For a State whose instrument of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession is deposited after the date this Agreement enters into force pursuant to paragraph (a) of this Article, this Agreement shall enter into force on the date of such deposit.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p352 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Upon entry into force of this Agreement pursuant to paragraph (a) of this Article, it may be applied provisionally with respect to any State whose Government signed it subject to ratification, acceptance or approval if that Government so requests at the time of signature or at any</SPAN></P>
<P class="p461 ft7">time thereafter prior to the entry into force of this Agreement. Provisional application shall terminate:</P>
<P class="p462 ft10">(i) upon deposit of an instrument of ratification, acceptance or approval of this Agreement by that Government;</P>
<P class="p463 ft7">(ii) upon expiration of two years from the date on which this Agreement enters into force without having been ratified, accepted or approved by that Government; or</P>
<P class="p464 ft10">(iii) upon notification by that Government, before expiration of the period mentioned in subparagraph (ii) of this paragraph, of its decision not to ratify, accept or approve this Agreement.</P>
<P class="p465 ft7">If provisional application terminates pursuant to subparagraph (ii) or (iii) of this paragraph, the provisions of paragraph (c) of Article XIV of this Agreement shall govern the rights and obligations of the Party</P>
<P class="p466 ft7">(d) Upon entry into force, this Agreement shall replace and terminate the Interim Agreement.</P>

<P class="p455 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Internal regulations for the executive organ shall provide for the prompt distribution to all Parties of copies of any ITSO document in accordance with their requests.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p469 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Consistent with the provisions of Resolution 1721 (XVI) of the General Assembly of the United Nations, the executive organ shall send to the Secretary General of the United Nations, and to the Specialized Agencies concerned, for their information, an annual report on the activities of ITSO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p470 ft7">Depositary</P>
<P class="p419 ft7">ARTICLE XX</P>
<P class="p471 ft90"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The Government of the United States of America shall be the Depositary for this Agreement, with which shall be deposited declarations made pursuant to paragraph (b) of Article XVII of this Agreement, instruments of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession, requests for provisional application, and notifications of ratification, acceptance or approval of amendments, of decisions to withdraw from ITSO, or of termination of the provisional application of this Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p325 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">This Agreement, of which the English, French and Spanish texts are equally authentic, shall be deposited in the archives of the Depositary. The Depositary shall transmit certified copies of the text of this Agreement to all Governments that have signed it or deposited instruments of accession to it, and to the International Telecommunication Union, and shall notify those Governments, and the International Telecommunication Union, of signatures, of declarations made pursuant to paragraph (b) of Article XVII of this Agreement, of the deposit of instruments of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession, of requests for provisional application, of commencement of the </SPAN><NOBR>sixty-day</NOBR> period referred to in paragraph (a) of Article XVIII of this Agreement, of the entry into force of this Agreement, of notifications of ratification, acceptance or approval of amendments, of the entry into force of amendments, of decisions to withdraw from ITSO, of withdrawals and of terminations of provisional application of this Agreement. Notice of the commencement of the <NOBR>sixty-day</NOBR> period shall be issued on the first day of that period.</P>
<P class="p472 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Upon entry into force of this Agreement, the Depositary shall register it with the Secretariat of the United Nations in accordance with Article 102 of the Charter of the United Nations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p473 ft7">Duration</P>
<P class="p448 ft7">ARTICLE XXI</P>
<P class="p474 ft98">This Agreement shall be in effect for at least twelve years from the date of transfer of ITSO’s space system to the Company. The Assembly of Parties may terminate this Agreement effective upon the twelfth anniversary of the date of transfer of ITSO’s space system to the Company</P>

<P class="p475 ft7">IN WITNESS WHEREOF the Plenipotentiaries gathered together in the city of Washington, who have submitted their full powers, found to be in good and due form, have signed this Agreement.</P>

<P class="p477 ft7">Provisions on Procedures Relating to Settlement of Disputes</P>
<P class="p478 ft7">ANNEX A</P>
<P class="p479 ft7">ARTICLE 1</P>
<P class="p480 ft7">The only disputants in arbitration proceedings instituted in accordance with this Annex shall be those referred to in Article XVI of this Agreement.</P>
<P class="p439 ft7">ARTICLE 2</P>
<P class="p481 ft7">An arbitral tribunal of three members duly constituted in accordance with the provisions of this Annex shall be competent to give a decision in any dispute cognizable pursuant to Article XVI of this Agreement.</P>
<P class="p482 ft7">ARTICLE 3</P>
<P class="p483 ft98">(a) Not later than sixty days before the opening date of the first and each subsequent ordinary meeting of the Assembly of Parties, each Party may submit to the executive organ the names of not more than two legal experts who will be available for the period from the end of such meeting until the end of the second subsequent ordinary meeting of the Assembly of Parties to serve as presidents or members of tribunals constituted in accordance with this Annex. From such nominees the executive organ shall prepare a list of all the persons thus nominated and shall attach to this list any biographical particulars submitted by the nominating Party, and shall distribute such list to all Parties not later than thirty days before the opening date of the meeting in question. If for any reason a nominee becomes unavailable for selection to the panel during the <NOBR>sixty-day</NOBR> period before the opening date of the meeting of the Assembly of Parties, the nominating Party may, not later than fourteen days before the</P>
<P class="p484 ft6">55</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_56">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t15">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">opening date of the meeting of the Assembly of Parties, substitute the name</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">of another legal expert.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p393 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">From the list mentioned in paragraph (a) of this Article, the Assembly of Parties shall select eleven persons to be members of a panel from which presidents of tribunals shall be selected, and shall select an alternate for each such member. Members and alternates shall serve for the period prescribed in paragraph (a) of this Article. If a member becomes unavailable to serve on the panel, he shall be replaced by his alternate.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p321 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">For the purpose of designating a chairman, the panel shall be convened to meet by the executive organ as soon as possible after the panel has been selected. Members of the panel may participate in this meeting in person, or through electronic means. The quorum for a meeting of the panel shall be nine of the eleven members. The panel shall designate one of its members as its chairman by a decision taken by the affirmative votes of at least six members, cast in one or, if necessary, more than one secret ballot. The chairman so designated shall hold office as chairman for the rest of his period of office as a member of the panel. The cost of the meeting of the panel shall be regarded as an administrative cost of ITSO.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p485 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">If both a member of the panel and the alternate for that member become unavailable to serve, the Assembly of Parties shall fill the vacancies thus created from the list referred to in paragraph (a) of this Article. A person selected to replace a member or alternate whose term of office has not expired shall hold office for the remainder of the term of his predecessor. Vacancies in the office of the chairman of the panel shall be filled by the panel by designation of one of its members in accordance with the procedure prescribed in paragraph (c) of this Article.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p486 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">In selecting the members of the panel and the alternates in accordance with paragraph (b) or (d) of this Article, the Assembly of Parties shall seek to ensure that the composition of the panel will always be able to reflect an adequate geographical representation, as well as the principal legal systems as they are represented among the Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p487 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">Any panel member or alternate serving on an arbitral tribunal at the expiration of his term shall continue to serve until the conclusion of any arbitral proceeding pending before such tribunal.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p439 ft7">ARTICLE 4</P>
<P class="p488 ft7">(a) Any petitioner wishing to submit a legal dispute to arbitration shall provide each respondent and the executive organ with a document which contains:</P>
<P class="p489 ft10">(i) a statement which fully describes the dispute being submitted for arbitration, the reasons why each respondent is required to participate in the arbitration, and the relief being requested;</P>
<P class="p490 ft90">(ii) a statement which sets forth why the subject matter of the dispute comes within the competence of a tribunal to be constituted in accordance with this Annex, and why the relief being requested can be granted by such tribunal if it finds in favor of the petitioner;</P>
<P class="p491 ft7">(iii) a statement explaining why the petitioner has been unable to achieve a settlement of the dispute within a reasonable time by negotiation or other means short of arbitration;</P>
<P class="p335 ft6">56</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_57">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t21">

<P class="p492 ft7">ARTICLE 5</P>
<P class="p493 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Within sixty days from the date copies of the document described in paragraph (a) of Article 4 of this Annex have been received by all the respondents, the side of the respondents shall designate an individual to serve as a member of the tribunal. Within that period, the respondents may, jointly or individually, provide each disputant and the executive organ with a document stating their responses to the document referred to in paragraph (a) of Article 4 of this Annex and including any </SPAN><NOBR>counter-claims</NOBR> arising out of the subject matter of the dispute. The executive organ shall promptly furnish the chairman of the panel with a copy of any such document.</P>
<P class="p451 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">In the event of a failure by the side of the respondents to make such a designation within the period allowed, the chairman of the panel shall make a designation from among the experts whose names were submitted to the executive organ pursuant to paragraph (a) of Article 3 of this Annex.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p450 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Within thirty days after the designation of the two members of the tribunal, they shall agree on a third person selected from the panel constituted in accordance with Article 3 of this Annex, who shall serve as the president of the tribunal. In the event of failure to reach agreement within such period of time, either of the two members designated may inform the chairman of the panel, who, within ten days, shall designate a member of the panel other than himself to serve as president of the tribunal.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p345 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The tribunal is constituted as soon as the president is</SPAN></P>
<P class="p65 ft7">selected.</P>
<P class="p492 ft7">ARTICLE 6</P>
<P class="p494 ft7">(a) If a vacancy occurs in the tribunal for reasons which the president or the remaining members of the tribunal decide are beyond the control of the disputants, or are compatible with the proper conduct of the arbitration proceedings, the vacancy shall be filled in accordance with the following provisions:</P>
<P class="p495 ft7">(i) if the vacancy occurs as a result of the withdrawal of a member appointed by a side to the dispute, then that side shall select a replacement within ten days after the vacancy occurs;</P>
<P class="p496 ft10">(ii) if the vacancy occurs as a result of the withdrawal of the president of the tribunal or of another member of the tribunal appointed by the chairman, a replacement shall be selected from the panel in</P>
<P class="p227 ft6">57</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_58">

	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">the manner described in paragraph (c) or (b) respectively of Article 5 of this</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">Annex.</SPAN> </TD>

<TR>
	<TD class="tr27 td102"><SPAN class="p355 ft7">ARTICLE 7</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr27 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p497 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The tribunal shall decide the date and place of its sittings.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p498 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The proceedings shall be held in private and all material presented to the tribunal shall be confidential, except that ITSO and the Parties who are disputants in the proceedings shall have the right to be present and shall have access to the material presented. When ITSO is a disputant in the proceedings, all Parties shall have the right to be present and shall have access to the material presented.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p499 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">In the event of a dispute over the competence of the tribunal, the tribunal shall deal with this question first, and shall give its decision as soon as possible.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p352 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The proceedings shall be conducted in writing, and each side shall have the right to submit written evidence in support of its allegations of fact and law. However, oral arguments and testimony may be given if the tribunal considers it appropriate.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p500 ft90"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The proceedings shall commence with the presentation of the case of the petitioner containing its arguments, related facts supported by evidence and the principles of law relied upon. The case of the petitioner shall be followed by the </SPAN><NOBR>counter-case</NOBR> of the respondent. The petitioner may submit a reply to the <NOBR>counter-case</NOBR> of the respondent. Additional pleadings shall be submitted only if the tribunal determines they are necessary.</P>
<P class="p501 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft95">The tribunal may hear and determine </SPAN><NOBR>counter-claims</NOBR> arising directly out of the subject matter of the dispute, provided the <NOBR>counter-claims</NOBR> are within its competence as defined in Article XVI of this Agreement.</P>
<P class="p502 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">If the disputants reach an agreement during the proceedings, the agreement shall be recorded in the form of a decision of the tribunal given by consent of the disputants.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p332 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">At any time during the proceedings, the tribunal may terminate the proceedings if it decides the dispute is beyond its competence as defined in Article XVI of the Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p330 ft7">(i)The deliberations of the tribunal shall be secret.</P>
<P class="p443 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(j)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">The decisions of the tribunal shall be presented in writing and shall be supported by a written opinion. Its rulings and decisions must be supported by at least two members. A member dissenting from the decision may submit a separate written opinion.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p503 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The tribunal shall forward its decision to the executive organ, which shall distribute it to all Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p403 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(l)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">The tribunal may adopt additional rules of procedure, consistent with those established by this Annex, which are necessary for the proceedings.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p507 ft7">ARTICLE 13</P>
<P class="p497 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The decision of the tribunal shall be based on</SPAN></P>
<P class="p347 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">this Agreement; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p346 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">generally accepted principles of law.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p508 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">The decision of the tribunal, including any reached by agreement of the disputants pursuant to paragraph (g) of Article 7 of this Annex, shall be binding on all the disputants and shall be carried out by them in good faith. In a case in which ITSO is a disputant, and the tribunal decides that a decision of one of its organs is null and void as not being authorized by or in compliance with this Agreement, the decision of the tribunal shall be binding on all Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p509 ft10"><SPAN class="ft10">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">In the event of a dispute as to the meaning or scope of its decision, the tribunal shall construe it at the request of any disputant.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p196 ft6">59</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_60">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p510 ft7">ARTICLE 14</P>
<P class="p511 ft98">Unless the tribunal determines otherwise because of the particular circumstances of the case, the expenses of the tribunal, including the remuneration of the members of the tribunal, shall be borne in equal shares by each side. Where a side consists of more than one disputant, the share of that side shall be apportioned by the tribunal among the disputants on that side. Where ITSO is a disputant, its expenses associated with the arbitration shall be regarded as an administrative cost of ITSO.</P>
<P class="p512 ft89">AMENDMENT TO THE OPERATING AGREEMENT</P>
<P class="p513 ft10">The only amendment involves Article 23 (Entry Into Force) of the Operating Agreement; all other provisions remain unchanged:</P>
<P class="p514 ft7">Entry Into Force</P>
<P class="p510 ft7">ARTICLE 23</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 2</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p515 ft7"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">This Operating Agreement shall enter into force for a Signatory on the date on which the Agreement enters into force, in accordance with paragraphs (a) and (d) or paragraphs (b) and (d) of Article XVIII of the Agreement, for the Party concerned.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p516 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">This Operating Agreement shall be applied provisionally for a Signatory on the date on which the Agreement is applied provisionally, in accordance with paragraphs (c) and (d) of Article XVIII of the Agreement, for the Party concerned.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p517 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">This Operating Agreement shall terminate either when the Agreement ceases to be in force or when amendments to the Agreement deleting references to the Operating Agreement enter into force, whichever is earlier.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p518 ft6">60</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<P class="p526 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft101">"Representatives" in the case of Parties to the Protocol, the Headquarters Party and Signatories, means representatives to Inmarsat and in each case means heads of delegations, alternates and advisers;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p527 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">"Archives" includes all manuscripts, correspondence, documents, photographs, films, optical and magnetic recordings, data recordings, graphic representations and computer programmes, belonging to or held by Inmarsat;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p528 ft6"><SPAN class="ft6">(j)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">"Official activities" of Inmarsat means activities carried out by the Organization in pursuance of its purpose as defined in the Convention and includes its administrative activities;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p529 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">"Expert" means a person other than a staff member appointed to carry out a specific task for or on behalf of Inmarsat and at its expense;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p530 ft6"><SPAN class="ft6">(l)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">“Inmarsat space segment” means the satellites, and tracking, telemetry, command, control, monitoring and related facilities and equipment required to support the operation of these satellites, which are owned or leased by Inmarsat;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p531 ft7"><SPAN class="ft6">(l)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft104">"Property" means anything that can be the subject of a right of ownership, including contractual rights.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p532 ft6">Article 2</P>
<P class="p533 ft6">Immunity of Inmarsat from Jurisdiction and Execution</P>
<P class="p534 ft6">(1) Unless it has expressly waived immunity in a particular case, Inmarsat shall, within the scope of its official activities, have immunity from jurisdiction except in respect of:</P>
<P class="p535 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">its commercial activities;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p536 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">a civil action by a third party for damage arising from an accident caused by a motor vehicle or other means of transport belonging to, or operated on behalf of,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p184 ft6">63</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_64">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t26">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td115"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Inmarsat, or in respect of a traffic offence involving</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td115"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">such means of transport;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 3</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p537 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">the attachment, pursuant to the final order of a court of law, of the salaries and emoluments, including pension rights, owed by Inmarsat to a staff member, or a former staff member;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p538 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">a </SPAN><NOBR>counter-claim</NOBR> directly connected with judicial proceedings initiated by Inmarsat.</P>
<P class="p539 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Notwithstanding paragraph (1), no action shall be brought in the courts of Parties to the Protocol against Inmarsat by Parties to the Convention, Signatories or persons acting for or deriving claims from any of them, relating to rights and obligations under the Convention or Operating Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p540 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">(a) The Inmarsat space segment, wherever located and by whomsoever held, shall be immune from any search, restraint, requisition, seizure, confiscation, expropriation, sequestration or execution, whether by executive, administrative or judicial action,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p541 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">All other property and assets of Inmarsat, wherever located and by whomsoever held, shall enjoy the immunity set out in paragraph (3)(a) except in respect of</SPAN></P>
<P class="p542 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">an attachment or execution in order to satisfy a final judgement or order of a court of law that relates to any proceedings that may be brought against Inmarsat pursuant to paragraph (1);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p543 ft6"><SPAN class="ft6">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">any action taken in accordance with the law of the State concerned which is temporarily necessary in connection with the prevention of and investigation into accidents involving motor vehicles or other means of transport belonging to, or operated on behalf of, Inmarsat;</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t27">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">(iiic)</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td116"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">expropriation in respect of real property for public</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft31">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td116"><SPAN class="p46 ft30">purposes and subject to prompt payment of fair</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td116"><SPAN class="p46 ft7">compensation, provided that such expropriation shall</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr6 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr6 td116"><SPAN class="p46 ft10">not prejudice the functions and operations of Inmarsat.</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr22 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr22 td116"><SPAN class="p544 ft6">Article 3</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr30 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr30 td116"><SPAN class="p545 ft6">Inviolability of Archives</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p546 ft6">The archives of Inmarsat shall be inviolable wherever located and by whomsoever held.</P>
