<DIV id="page_65">


<P class="p22 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p22 ft6">Bilaga 3</P>
<P class="p548 ft6">Article 4</P>
<P class="p549 ft6">Exemption from Taxes and Duties</P>
<P class="p550 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft109">Within the scope of its official activities, Inmarsat and its property and income shall be exempt from all national direct and other taxes not normally incorporated in the price of goods and services.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p551 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">If Inmarsat, within the scope of its official activities, acquires goods or uses services of substantial value, and if the price of these goods or services includes taxes or duties, Parties to the Protocol shall, whenever possible, take appropriate measures to remit or reimburse the amount of such taxes or duties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p161 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Within the scope of its official activities, Inmarsat shall be exempt from customs duties, taxes and related charges on the Inmarsat space segment and on equipment connected with the launching of satellites for use in the Inmarsat space segment.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p552 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Goods acquired by Inmarsat within the scope of its official activities shall be exempt from all prohibitions and restrictions on import or export.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p553 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(5)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">No exemption shall be accorded in respect of taxes and duties which represent charges for specific services rendered.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p554 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(6)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">No exemption shall be accorded in respect of goods acquired by, or services provided to, Inmarsat for the personal benefit of staff members.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p555 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(7)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Goods exempted under this Article shall not be transferred, hired out or lent, permanently or temporarily, or sold, except in accordance with conditions laid down by the Party to the Protocol which granted the exemption.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p556 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(8)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft109">Payments from Inmarsat to Signatories, pursuant to the Operating Agreement, shall be exempt from national taxes by any Party to the Protocol, other than the Party which has designated the Signatory.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p557 ft6">Article 5</P>
<P class="p558 ft6">Funds, Currency and Securities</P>
<P class="p559 ft6">Inmarsat may receive and hold any kind of funds, currency or securities and dispose of them freely for any of its official activities. It may hold accounts in any currency to the extent required to meet its obligations.</P>
<P class="p560 ft6">65</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_66">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t28">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td117"><SPAN class="p561 ft30">Article 6</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td117"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 3</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr23 td117"><SPAN class="p562 ft6">Official Communications and Publications</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr23 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p563 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">With regard to its official communications and transfer of all its documents, Inmarsat shall enjoy in the territory of each Party to the Protocol treatment not less favourable than that generally accorded to equivalent intergovernmental organizations in the matter of priorities, rates and taxes on mails and all forms of telecommunications, as far as may be compatible with any international agreements to which that Party to the Protocol is a party.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p564 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">With regard to its official communications, Inmarsat may employ all appropriate means of communication, including messages in code or cipher. Parties to the Protocol shall not impose any restriction on the official communications of Inmarsat or on the circulation of its official publications. No censorship shall be applied to such communications and publications.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p565 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Inmarsat may install and use a radio transmitter only with the consent of the Party to the Protocol concerned.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p566 ft6">Article 7</P>
<P class="p567 ft6">Staff Members</P>
<P class="p568 ft6">(1) Staff members shall enjoy the following privileges and immunities:</P>
<P class="p569 ft19"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft111">immunity from jurisdiction, even after they have left the service of Inmarsat, in respect of acts, including words spoken or written, done by them in the exercise of their official functions; this immunity shall not, however, apply in the case of a traffic offence committed by a staff member, or in the case of damage caused by a motor vehicle or other means of transport belonging to or driven by him;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p570 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">exemption, together with members of their families forming part of their respective households, from any obligations in respect of national service, including military service;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">inviolability for all their official papers related to the exercise of their functions within the scope of the official activities of Inmarsat;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p572 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft101">exemption, together with members of their families forming part of their respective households, from immigration restrictions and alien registration;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p184 ft6">66</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_67">


<P class="p22 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p573 ft6">(e) the same treatment in the matter of currency and Bilaga 3 exchange control as is accorded to staff members of intergovernmental organizations;</P>
<P class="p574 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft112">together with members of their families forming part of their respective households, the same facilities as to repatriation in time of international crisis as are accorded to staff members of intergovernmental organizations;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p575 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft101">the right to import free of duty their furniture and personal effects, including a motor vehicle, at the time of first taking up their post in the State concerned, and the right to export them free of duty on termination of their functions in that State, in both cases in accordance with the laws and regulations of the State concerned. However, except in accordance with such laws and regulations, goods which have been exempted under this </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraph</NOBR> shall not be transferred, hired out or lent, permanently or temporarily, or sold.</P>
<P class="p576 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft109">Salaries and emoluments paid by Inmarsat to staff members shall be exempt from income tax from the date upon which such staff members have begun to be liable for a tax imposed on their salaries by Inmarsat for the latter's benefit. Parties to the Protocol may take these salaries and emoluments into account for the purpose of assessing the amount of taxes to be applied to income from other sources. Parties to the Protocol are not required to grant exemption from income tax in respect of pensions and annuities paid to former staff members.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p577 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">Provided that staff members are covered by an Inmarsat’s social security scheme, Inmarsat and its staff members shall be exempt from all compulsory contributions to national social security schemes. This exemption does not preclude any voluntary participation in a national social security scheme in accordance with the law of the Party to the Protocol concerned; neither does it oblige a Party to the Protocol to make payments of benefits under social security schemes to staff members who are exempt under the provisions of this paragraph.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p578 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The Parties to the Protocol shall not be obliged to accord to their nationals or permanent residents the privileges and immunities referred to in </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraphs</NOBR> (b), (d), (e), (f) and (g) of paragraph (1).</P>
<P class="p579 ft6">Article 8</P>
<P class="p580 ft6">Director General</P>
<P class="p504 ft6">67</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_68">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t1">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td118"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">(1)</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td119"><SPAN class="p54 ft6">In addition to the privileges and immunities provided for staff</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">members under Article 7, the Director General shall enjoy:</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 3</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p581 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">immunity from arrest and detention;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p582 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">immunity from civil and administrative jurisdiction and execution enjoyed by diplomatic agents, except in the case of damage caused by a motor vehicle or other means of transport belonging to or driven by him;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p583 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft111">full immunity from criminal jurisdiction, except in the case of a traffic offence caused by a motor vehicle or other means of transport belonging to, or driven by him, subject to </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraph</NOBR> (a) above.</P>
<P class="p584 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">The Parties to the Protocol shall not be obliged to accord to their nationals or permanent residents the immunities referred to in this Article.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p579 ft6">Article 9</P>
<P class="p585 ft6">Representatives of Parties</P>
<P class="p586 ft19">(1) Representatives of the Parties to the Protocol and representatives of the Headquarters Party shall enjoy, while exercising their official functions and in the course of their journeys to and from their place of meeting, the following privileges and immunities:</P>
<P class="p581 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">immunity from any form of arrest or detention pending</SPAN></P>
<P class="p183 ft6">trial;</P>
<P class="p587 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">immunity from jurisdiction, even after the termination of their mission, in respect of acts, including words spoken or written, done by them in the exercise of their official functions; however, there shall be no immunity in the case of a traffic offence committed by a representative, or in the case of damage caused by a motor vehicle or other means of transport belonging to or driven by him;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p588 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">inviolability for all their official papers;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p589 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft101">exemption, together with members of their families forming part of their respective households, from immigration restrictions and alien registration;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p590 ft44"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft113">the same treatment in the matter of currency and exchange control as is accorded to representatives of foreign governments on temporary official missions;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p591 ft6">68</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_69">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t25">

	<TD class="tr0 td113"><SPAN class="p46 ft7">their personal luggage as is accorded to representatives</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 3</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td114"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td113"><SPAN class="p46 ft6">of foreign governments on temporary official missions.</SPAN> </TD>

</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p592 ft6">(2) The provisions of paragraph (1) shall not apply in relations between a Party to the Protocol and its representatives. Further, the provisions of paragraphs (a), (d), (e) and (f) of paragraph (1) shall not apply in relations between a Party to the Protocol and its nationals or permanent residents.</P>
<P class="p593 ft6">Article 10</P>
<P class="p594 ft6">Representatives of Signatories</P>
<P class="p595 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Representatives of Signatories and representatives of the Signatory of the Headquarters Party shall, while exercising their official functions in relation to the work of Inmarsat and in the course of their journeys to and from their place of meeting, enjoy the following privileges and immunities:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p596 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">immunity from jurisdiction, even after the termination of their mission, in respect of acts, including words spoken or written, done by them in the exercise of their official functions; however, there shall be no immunity in the case of a traffic offence committed by a representative, or in the case of damage caused by a motor vehicle or other means of transport belonging to or driven by him;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p597 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">inviolability for all their official papers;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p598 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft113">exemption, together with members of their families forming part of their respective households, from immigration restrictions and alien registration.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p599 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The provisions of paragraph (1) shall not apply in relations between a Party to the Protocol and the representative of the Signatory designated by it. Further, the provisions of </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraph</NOBR> (c) of paragraph (1) shall not apply in relations between a Party to the Protocol and its nationals or permanent residents.</P>
<P class="p600 ft6">Article 11</P>
<P class="p601 ft6">Experts</P>
<P class="p602 ft6">(1) Experts, while exercising their official functions in relation to the work of Inmarsat, and in the course of their journeys to and from the place of their missions, shall enjoy the following privileges and immunities:</P>

<P class="p581 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">inviolability for all their official papers;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p603 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">the same treatment in the matter of currency and exchange control as is accorded to the staff members of intergovernmental organizations;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p572 ft44"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft101">exemption, together with members of their families forming part of their respective households, from immigration restrictions and alien registration;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p604 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">the same facilities as regards their personal luggage as are accorded to experts of other intergovernmental organizations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p605 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The Parties to the Protocol shall not be obliged to accord to their nationals or permanent residents the privileges and immunities referred to in </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraphs</NOBR> (c), (d), and (e) of paragraph (1).</P>
<P class="p606 ft6">Article 12</P>
<P class="p607 ft6">Notification of Staff Members and Experts</P>
<P class="p608 ft6">The Director General of Inmarsat shall at least once every year notify the Parties to the Protocol of the names and nationalities of the staff members and experts to whom the provisions of Articles 7, 8 and 11 apply.</P>
<P class="p609 ft6">Article 13</P>
<P class="p610 ft6">Waiver</P>
<P class="p611 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The privileges, exemptions and immunities provided for in this Protocol are not granted for the personal benefit of individuals but for the efficient performance of their official functions.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p612 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">If, in the view of the authorities listed below, privileges and immunities are likely to impede the course of justice, and in all cases where they may be waived without prejudice to the purposes for which they have been accorded, these authorities have the right and duty to waive such privileges and immunities:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p613 ft44"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft113">the Parties to the Protocol in respect of their representatives and representatives of their Signatories;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p184 ft6">70</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_71">


<P class="p22 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p573 ft6">(b) the Council in respect of the Director General of Bilaga 3 Inmarsat;</P>
<P class="p614 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">the Director General of Inmarsat in respect of staff members and experts.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p615 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">the Assembly, convened if necessary in extraordinary session, in respect of Inmarsat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p606 ft6">Article 14</P>
<P class="p616 ft6">Assistance to Individuals</P>
<P class="p617 ft6">The Parties to the Protocol shall take all appropriate measures to facilitate entry, stay and departure of representatives, staff members and experts.</P>
<P class="p606 ft6">Article 15</P>
<P class="p618 ft6">Observance of Laws and Regulations</P>
<P class="p619 ft6">Inmarsat, and all persons enjoying privileges and immunities under this Protocol, shall, without prejudice to the other provisions thereof, respect the laws and regulations of the Parties to the Protocol concerned and cooperate at all times with the competent authorities of those Parties in order to ensure the observance of their laws and regulations.</P>
<P class="p620 ft6">Article 16</P>
<P class="p621 ft6">Precautionary Measures</P>
<P class="p622 ft90">Each Party to the Protocol retains the right to take all precautionary measures necessary in the interest of its security.</P>
<P class="p620 ft6">Article 17</P>
<P class="p623 ft6">Settlement of Disputes</P>
<P class="p624 ft44">Any dispute between Parties to the Protocol or between Inmarsat and a Party to the Protocol concerning the interpretation or application of the Protocol shall be settled by negotiation or by some other agreed method. If the dispute is not settled within twelve (12) months, the parties concerned may, by common agreement, refer the dispute for</P>
<P class="p61 ft6">decision to a tribunal of three arbitrators. One of these arbitrators shall</P>
<P class="p184 ft6">71</P>

<DIV id="page_72">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t1">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">be chosen by each of the parties to the dispute, and the third, who shall</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">be the Chairman of the tribunal, shall be chosen by the first two</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 3</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">arbitrators. Should the first two arbitrators fail to agree upon the third</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft7">within two months of their own appointment, the third arbitrator shall be</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p620 ft6">Article 18</P>
<P class="p625 ft6">Complementary Agreements</P>
<P class="p626 ft6">Inmarsat may conclude with any Party to the Protocol complementary agreements to give effect to the provisions of this Protocol as regards such Party to the Protocol to ensure the efficient functioning of Inmarsat.</P>
<P class="p606 ft6">Article 19</P>
<P class="p627 ft6">Signature, Ratification and Accession</P>
<P class="p628 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">This Protocol shall be open for signature at London from 1 December 1981 to 31 May 1982.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p629 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">All Parties to the Convention, other than the Headquarters Party, may become Parties to this Protocol by:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p535 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">signature not subject to ratification, acceptance or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p331 ft6">approval; or</P>
<P class="p630 ft10"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft114">signature subject to ratification, acceptance or approval, followed by ratification, acceptance or approval; or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p597 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">accession.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p631 ft90"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft115">Ratification, acceptance, approval or accession shall be effected by the deposit of the appropriate instrument with the Depositary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p632 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">Reservations to this Protocol may be made in accordance with international law.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p606 ft6">Article 20</P>
<P class="p633 ft6">Entry into Force and Duration of Protocol</P>
<P class="p634 ft6">72</P>
</DIV>

<P class="p61 ft6">to be in force.</P>
<P class="p635 ft6">Article 21</P>
<P class="p636 ft6">Entry into Force and Duration for a State</P>
<P class="p637 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">For a State which has fulfilled the requirements of paragraph (2) of Article 19 after the date of entry into force of this Protocol, the Protocol shall enter into force on the thirtieth day after the date of signature or of the deposit of such instrument with the Depositary respectively.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p159 ft19"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">Any Party to the Protocol may denounce this Protocol by giving written notice to the Depositary. The denunciation shall become effective twelve (12) months after the date of receipt of the notice by the Depositary or such longer period as may be specified in the notice.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p638 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">A Party to the Protocol shall cease to be a Party to the Protocol on the date that it ceases to be a Party to the Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p620 ft6">Article 22</P>
<P class="p639 ft6">Depositary</P>
<P class="p640 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">The Director General of Inmarsat shall be the Depositary of this Protocol.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p641 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">The Depositary shall, in particular, promptly notify all Parties to the Convention of:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p642 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">any signature of the Protocol;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p643 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">the deposit of any instrument of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p535 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">the date of entry into force of this Protocol;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p535 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">the date when a State has ceased to be a Party to this</SPAN></P>
<P class="p65 ft6">Protocol;</P>
<P class="p535 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">any other communications relating to this Protocol.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p644 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Upon entry into force of this Protocol, the Depositary shall transmit a certified copy of the original to the Secretariat of the</SPAN></P>
<P class="p227 ft6">73</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_74">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t1">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">United Nations for registration and publication in accordance with</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Article 102 of the Charter of the United Nations.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 3</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p606 ft6">Article 23</P>
<P class="p645 ft6">Authentic Texts</P>
<P class="p646 ft17">This Protocol is established in a single original in the English, French, Russian and Spanish languages, all the texts being equally authentic, and shall be deposited with the Director General of Inmarsat who shall send a certified copy to each Party to the Convention.</P>
<P class="p647 ft7">IN WITNESS WHEREOF the undersigned, duly authorized for that purpose by their respective Governments, have signed this Protocol.</P>
<P class="p648 ft6">DONE AT LONDON this first day of December one thousand nine hundred and eighty one.</P>
<P class="p649 ft6">[Signatures omitted]</P>

<P class="p22 ft6">Bilaga 4</P>
<P class="p652 ft7">AMENDING AGREEMENT TO THE PROTOCOL ON THE</P>
<P class="p653 ft7">PRIVILEGES AND IMMUNITIES OF THE INTERNATIONAL</P>
<P class="p654 ft7">MOBILE SATELLITE ORGANIZATION</P>
<P class="p655 ft6">THE PARTIES TO THE PRESENT AGREEMENT:</P>
<P class="p279 ft117">BEING PARTIES to the Convention on the International Mobile Satellite Organization (formerly the International Maritime Satellite Organization (INMARSAT)), as amended, (“the Convention”);</P>
<P class="p279 ft117">ALSO BEING PARTIES to the Protocol on the Privileges and Immunities of the International Mobile Satellite Organization (Inmarsat), done at London on 1 December 1981 (“the Protocol”);</P>
<P class="p279 ft118">TAKING NOTE that the Inmarsat Assembly of Parties, at its Twelfth Session, adopted further amendments to the Convention for the restructuring of the Organization, including amendments to Article 26(4) thereof pursuant to which the Protocol was concluded;</P>
<P class="p181 ft119">CONSIDERING that it is desirable to amend the Protocol for consistency with the amended Convention;</P>
<P class="p156 ft6">HAVE AGREED TO AMEND THE PROTOCOL AS FOLLOWS:</P>
<P class="p656 ft6">Article I</P>
<P class="p657 ft6">The title of the Protocol is replaced with the following :</P>
<P class="p658 ft6">PROTOCOL ON THE PRIVILEGES AND IMMUNITIES OF THE INTERNATIONAL MOBILE SATELLITE ORGANIZATION</P>
<P class="p659 ft6">Article II</P>
<P class="p182 ft119">The preambular paragraphs of the Protocol are replaced by the following text:</P>
<P class="p660 ft120">HAVING REGARD to the Convention on the International Mobile Satellite Organization, opened for signature at London on</P>
<P class="p661 ft6">75</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_76">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p84 ft119">3 September 1976, as amended, and, in particular, to Article 9(6) of the amended Convention;</P>
<P class="p662 ft117">TAKING NOTE that the Organization will conclude a Headquarters Agreement with the Government of the United Kingdom of Great Britain and Northern Ireland on 15 April 1999.</P>
<P class="p663 ft117">CONSIDERING that the aim of this Protocol is to facilitate the achievement of the purpose of the Organization and to ensure the efficient performance of its functions;</P>
<P class="p664 ft6">Article III</P>
<P class="p665 ft6">Article 1 - Use of Terms - is replaced by the following text:</P>
<P class="p666 ft6">Use of Terms</P>
<P class="p667 ft6">For the purposes of this Protocol:</P>
<P class="p668 ft122"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft121">"Convention" means the Convention on the International Mobile Satellite Organization, including its Annex, opened for signature at London on 3 September 1976, as amended;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p669 ft120"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft123">"Party to the Convention" means a State for which the Convention is in force;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p670 ft119"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft124">“Organization” means the International Mobile Satellite Organization;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p671 ft7"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">"Headquarters Party" means the Party to the Convention in</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t29">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr12 td120"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">whose territory</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr12 td121"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">the Organization has established its</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td120"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">headquarters;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td121"><SPAN class="p2 ft9">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p672 ft117"><SPAN class="ft10">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft125">"Party to the Protocol" means a State for which this Protocol, or this Protocol as amended, as the case may be, is in force;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p673 ft117"><SPAN class="ft7">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft126">"Staff member" means the Director and any person employed full time by the Organization and subject to its staff regulations;</SPAN></P>
</DIV>

<P class="p674 ft118"><SPAN class="ft7">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft127">"Representatives" in the case of Parties to the Protocol, and the Headquarters Party, means representatives to the Organization and in each case means heads of delegations, alternates and advisers;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p669 ft118"><SPAN class="ft7">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft127">"Archives" includes all manuscripts, correspondence, documents, photographs, films, optical and magnetic recordings, data recordings, graphic representations and computer programmes, belonging to or held by the Organization;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p669 ft118"><SPAN class="ft7">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft128">"Official activities" of the Organization means activities carried out by the Organization in pursuance of its purpose as defined in the Convention and includes its administrative activities;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p669 ft117"><SPAN class="ft6">(j)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft129">"Expert" means a person other than a staff member appointed to carry out a specific task for or on behalf of the Organization and at its expense;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p673 ft120"><SPAN class="ft7">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft123">"Property" means anything that can be the subject of a right of ownership, including contractual rights.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p185 ft117"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft134">The privileges, exemptions and immunities provided for in this Protocol are not granted for the personal benefit of individuals but for the efficient performance of their official functions.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p204 ft118"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft127">If, in the view of the authorities listed below, privileges and immunities are likely to impede the course of justice, and in all cases where they may be waived without prejudice to the purposes for which they have been accorded, these authorities have the right and duty to waive such privileges and immunities:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p715 ft119"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft124">the Parties to the Protocol in respect of their representatives;</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p39 ft6">(2) All Parties to the Convention, other than the Headquarters Party,</P>
<P class="p735 ft6">may become Parties to this Amending Agreement by:</P>
<P class="p736 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">signature not subject to ratification, acceptance or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p737 ft6">approval; or</P>
<P class="p668 ft136"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft137">signature subject to ratification, acceptance or approval, followed by ratification, acceptance or approval; or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p736 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">accession.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p738 ft139"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft138">Ratification, acceptance, approval or accession shall be effected by the deposit of the appropriate instrument with the Depositary.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p700 ft118"><SPAN class="ft7">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft127">A State which is a Party to this Amending Agreement but is not a Party to the Protocol shall be bound by the provisions of the Protocol as amended by this Amending Agreement in relation to other Parties hereto, but shall not be bound by the provisions of the Protocol in relation to States Parties only to the Protocol.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p212 ft120"><SPAN class="ft7">(5)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft123">Reservations to this Amending Agreement may be made in accordance with international law.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 4</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p363 ft6">Article XXIV</P>
<P class="p739 ft6">Entry into Force of Amending Agreement</P>
<P class="p181 ft117">This Amending Agreement shall enter into force on the thirtieth day after the date on which two Parties to the Convention have fulfilled the requirements of paragraph (2) of Article XXIII.</P>
<P class="p740 ft6">Article XXV</P>
<P class="p741 ft6">Entry into Force for a State</P>
<P class="p182 ft118">(1) For a State which has fulfilled the requirements of paragraph (2) of Article XXIII after the date of entry into force of this Amending Agreement, this Amending Agreement shall enter into force on the thirtieth day after the date of signature or of the deposit of such instrument with the Depositary respectively.</P>
<P class="p742 ft6">83</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_84">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p39 ft6">(2) Any State which becomes a Party to the Protocol after the entry</P>
<P class="p735 ft6">into force of this Amending Agreement pursuant to Article XXIV shall,</P>
<P class="p735 ft6">failing an expression of a different intention by that State:</P>
<P class="p203 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">be considered as a Party to the Protocol as amended; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p743 ft117"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft134">be considered as a Party to the unamended Protocol in relation to any Party to the Protocol not bound by this Amending Agreement.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p39 ft6">Prop. 2003/04:29</P>
<P class="p39 ft6">Bilaga 4</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p363 ft6">Article XXVI</P>
<P class="p744 ft6">Depositary</P>
<P class="p182 ft119"><SPAN class="ft7">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft131">The Director of the Organization shall be the Depositary of this Amending Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p687 ft120"><SPAN class="ft7">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft123">The Depositary shall, in particular, promptly notify all Parties to the Convention of:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p745 ft6"><SPAN class="ft10">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">any signature of the Amending Agreement;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p746 ft120"><SPAN class="ft7">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft135">the deposit of any instrument of ratification, acceptance, approval or accession;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p745 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">the date of entry into force of this Amending Agreement;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p747 ft6"><SPAN class="ft7">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft107">any other communications relating to this Amending</SPAN></P>
<P class="p748 ft6">Agreement .</P>
<P class="p681 ft118"><SPAN class="ft7">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft127">Upon entry into force of this Amending Agreement, the Depositary shall transmit a certified copy of the original to the Secretariat of the United Nations for registration and publication in accordance with Article 102 of the Charter of the United Nations.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p749 ft6">Article XXVII</P>
<P class="p750 ft6">Authentic Texts</P>
<P class="p751 ft136">This Amending Agreement is established in a single original in the English, French, Russian and Spanish languages, all the texts being</P>
<P class="p752 ft40">equally authentic, and shall be deposited with the Director of the</P>
<P class="p184 ft6">84</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_85">


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t1">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Organization who shall send a certified copy to each Party to the</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft10">Prop. 2003/04:29</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td102"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Convention.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td64"><SPAN class="p2 ft6">Bilaga 4</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p753 ft117">IN WITNESS WHEREOF the undersigned, duly authorized for that purpose by their respective Governments, have signed this Amending Agreement.</P>
<P class="p754 ft120">DONE AT LONDON this 25th day of September one thousand nine hundred and ninety eight.</P>
